msg:Sheraton Xiamen blew all expectations!

What an amazingly relaxing and enjoyable stay it was. The team members are exceptional.

Carrie especially gave wonderful advice on exploring the art districts, Bruce was swift with essential ferry information, and Jason was cheerful in sharing locations of coffee shops and parks. The Sheraton team are thoughtful and passionate, I was amazed by the warmth at this hotel.

Beautiful scenery surrounds the location and it is easy to arrive at the major destinations that many people come to Xiamen to see. The grounds, in which the hotel stands, are vibrant with plantations and trees, making the area a wonderful finishing point for evening walks. The rooms are inviting, clean and comfortable.

The facilities, overall, were much better than expected. There is a sauna, which was a surprise, I missed that detail in booking. Gym equipment is new and runs smoothly, it seems the pool is much enjoyed by families and solo people alike.

I did not eat at the hotel, but I could clearly see there is a great deal of choice on offer at the buffet breakfast.

When I revisit Xiamen I will gladly return to the Sheraton Xiamen.

When I first read reviews about the water temperature in the bathroom, it was said that the water temperature was not enough. I adjusted the temperature on the right to 38¬∞C and turned on the left to the maximum water volume. In this way, the water temperature was just right. good.
I felt a little stuffy when I first entered the room, so I asked the waiter to help open the window, and it was much better!

Without thinking, I was directly given room 1704. I raised questions (so many floors and rooms, can you give me a room without 4?), but he did not reflect on it and first argued that this was the only room on the 17th floor. After that, he solved the problem by "getting angry" and gave me room 1708.
He also questioned that the room I booked with breakfast was "wrong", meaning that I cheated. We booked hotels on the APP, so how could it be the customer's turn to cheat? If there is a chance to cheat, it is only the business that has the opportunity to cheat. I booked early, and it is very likely that I saw that the room rate at that time was higher than what I booked, and I felt that I lost money. Is this the style of a five-star hotel? ? ? ! ! ! However, when the breakfast is worth 168 yuan, it is not worth it. In addition, the canned fruit is scattered in a glass jar and then placed on ice. It ferments, has small bubbles, and tastes sour.
The hotel's buffet from Thursday to Sunday, dinner is 179. I can only suggest: if you have time to go out, you should eat outside. You will be disappointed. Many parts are similar or the same as breakfast.

In fact, problems with hotel facilities and catering do not necessarily make people feel dissatisfied. But the problem of service attitude is something that can be directly withdrawn and directly felt by residents.
Finally, I emphasize again: I strongly complain about the boy who received the front desk at around 8:30 pm on April 3! ! !

posted:Posted March 14, 2023
msg:An old money Sheraton with "story" and no "accident" üí∞
I stayed in Xiamen for one night on a temporary business trip. In contrast, I chose Sheraton because it was the most cost-effective. Surprisingly, he gave me an experience that exceeded my expectations.
First of all, the service staff is very professional and reliable. From the front desk to the concierge to the guest room to the restaurant, all the service staff will remember you and provide services with your surname, making you feel that you are being cared for meticulously and respected politely. This is actually a requirement that I had never expected from Sheraton, and even some high-end hotels may not have such standard and considerate details, so although this time is short-lived, it made me feel unexpectedly warm.
Then come the guest rooms. Older hotels will inevitably leave some mottled "accidents" in the guest rooms, but fortunately, Sheraton's guest rooms only have "stories". Although the facilities are not up-to-date, it can be seen that they are carefully maintained and managed, including carpets and furniture, which are brand new and not old. The bedding is comfortable and the pillows can be obtained from the room service staff according to the needs. Even if you sleep on an unfamiliar bed, he can create a familiar sense of comfort for you.
Finally, there is one thing to praise, and that is the socket. üëçüèªGenerally, the layout of sockets in such old money hotels will be limited by hardware, which cannot meet everyone‚Äôs charging needs, especially when going out, it is inevitable that you will forget this plug and which data cable. But the caring Sheraton has prepared multi-interface/three-dimensional sockets at the head of the bed to meet the charging needs of digital products with different devices and ports. It is sometimes a simple but rare thing to easily and conveniently charge at the bedside without looking for the hotel socket like hide-and-seek.
All kinds of experiences have left me with a deep impression on Sheraton. I believe that if I have the opportunity to stay for a long time, I will definitely have a different feeling. I look forward to my next stay!
